## Entry Template

| Batch | Scope | Owner | Reviewer | Status | Verification | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `Batch N` | short summary | implementer | reviewer | `planned`, `implemented`, `reviewed`, or `changes-requested` | exact commands, success/failure, and the targeted artifact or behavior confirmed | follow-ups |

Notes must record the second-pass disposition explicitly once it runs, for example
`second-pass: approved` or `second-pass: changes-requested`.
The latest reviewed batch note should also carry the next-batch recommendation explicitly.
Global scheduling is governed by the `R0` track scheduler in
`docs/full-amflow-completion-roadmap.md`; per-row next-batch recommendations are local suggestions
inside the active track, not the authoritative global order.

Public `RunEtaGeneratedReduction(...)` / `BuildEtaGeneratedDESystem(...)` remain live-reducer helpers, and direct `SolveEtaGeneratedSeries(...)`, invariant-generated wrappers, direct `SolveDifferentialEquation(...)`, and other non-wrapper entry points stay unchanged. This landed row is the reviewed wrapper-only `SkipReduction` slice used by `Milestone M4`; broader helper/public `SkipReduction` semantics remain deferred |

## Review Checklist

- Confirm the edited batch only touched its declared file ownership.
- Confirm the manifest/schema and docs match the actual bootstrap behavior.
- Confirm `references/snapshots/amflow/prefactor_convention_lock.md` stays synchronized with
  `specs/amflow-prefactor-reference.yaml` for provenance, normalized literals, and explicit
  non-claims.
- Confirm `ResolveEtaMode(...)` validates the full supplied user-defined registry for null entries, duplicate names, and builtin-name collisions before any lookup proceeds.
- Confirm scripts handle dry-run and non-dry-run modes cleanly.
- Confirm placeholder goldens are metadata-only and do not claim real parity.
- Confirm reruns of the fetch helper verify the AMFlow remote and refresh the requested ref before pinning.
- Confirm tar extraction rejects symlink, hardlink, device, absolute-path, and escaping entries before any payload is written.
- Confirm reruns of the golden freezer refresh placeholder-managed files without escaping the phase-0 layout.
- Confirm the Kira runner records command text, exit code, stdout/stderr log paths, and environment overrides for every run attempt.
- Confirm the Kira runner also records the execution working directory for every run attempt.
- Confirm repeated Kira runs allocate unique attempt-scoped log files and do not overwrite prior attempts.
- Confirm the Kira runner rejects invalid or missing executable paths without attempting execution.
- Confirm invalid-configuration paths still materialize deterministic stdout/stderr logs.
- Confirm preparation-file writes are checked and required emitted files are validated before execution.
- Confirm pre-exec startup failures are classified as `FailedToStart` and not collapsed into completed exit-code results.
- Confirm fake-executable tests cover both successful and failing Kira exits without requiring a real reducer install.
- Confirm `results/<family>/masters` parsing uses the first token per line and rejects malformed or duplicate master labels deterministically.
- Confirm `results/<family>/kira_target.m` parsing is linear-in-masters only, rejects malformed rules and unknown masters, and appends master identity rules deterministically.
- Confirm parsed reduction rules canonicalize duplicate master coefficients and drop zero-net rules deterministically.
- Confirm missing or empty `kira_target.m` falls back to identity rules over the parsed master basis.
- Confirm DE assembly uses only explicit reduced derivative rules and never satisfies derivative-target lookup from the appended identity-rule tail.
- Confirm DE assembly row bindings are explicit, cover the canonical master basis in exact order, and reject row permutations locally.
- Confirm DE assembly rejects derivative-target arity mismatches, missing reduced targets, and master-basis mismatches before constructing a `DESystem`.
- Confirm `ValidateDESystem` rejects duplicate variable names, extra undeclared matrix keys, and coefficient matrices whose row or column counts do not match the master basis.
- Confirm `EtaInsertionDecision` carries propagator indices and builtin mode `All` selects all non-auxiliary propagators by index.
- Confirm `ApplyEtaInsertion(...)` rewrites only the selected propagators, appends `eta` to invariants exactly once, preserves the input spec, and preserves non-expression propagator metadata.
- Confirm eta insertion rejects empty selections, duplicate indices, out-of-range indices, selected auxiliary propagators, and selected nonzero-mass propagators deterministically.
- Confirm builtin eta modes beyond the accepted narrow set stay honest: reviewed `All` remains the baseline selector, landed `Prescription` remains only a bootstrap alias over `All`, landed `Propagator` remains only the reviewed structural selector on `main`, landed `Mass` remains only the narrow local equal-nonzero selector plus selected-propagator outer-whitespace trim on rewritten mass literals, accepted `Batch 50a` remains only internal blocker telemetry on `main`, and landed `Batch 50b` on current `main` remains only an internal topology-prerequisite bridge/prereq snapshot; on landed `main`, still-unaccepted builtin modes such as `Branch` and `Loop` fail deterministically without silently picking a placeholder propagator. Current local worktree (`Batch 50`) adds supported single-top-sector squared-linear-momentum selector semantics; see `src/runtime/eta_mode.cpp:819-863`.
- Confirm eta derivative generation uses the reviewed auxiliary-family transform, emits `-ai * J(...,ai+1,...)` only for rewritten propagators with `ai != 0`, and preserves deduplicated reduction-target order.
- Confirm eta derivative generation rejects master family mismatches and master-index arity mismatches against the transformed family.
- Confirm invariant derivative generation consumes explicit same-family denominator-derivative expressions, adds factor indices onto the shifted master indices, combines duplicate row targets in encounter order, preserves deduplicated global target order, and rejects variable-kind/family/arity mismatches deterministically.
- Confirm `BuildInvariantDerivativeSeed(...)` derives one invariant seed from the accepted bootstrap `ProblemSpec` subset without mutating the input spec, preserves propagator-table arity, ignores numeric substitutions, and rejects unsupported grammar, missing scalar-product data, unknown momenta, unsupported propagator kinds, and non-representable derivative terms deterministically.
- Confirm generated-row assembly uses only explicit parsed reduction rules, rejects identity-fallback reductions when generated targets need explicit rules, and composes matrix entries as literal `(<generated coeff>)*(<reduction coeff>)` strings without simplification.
- Confirm `PrepareForTargets(...)` preserves explicit target order exactly and leaves `Prepare(...)` unchanged on `ProblemSpec.targets`.
- Confirm explicit-target Kira preparation rejects empty, duplicate, family-mismatched, and arity-mismatched override targets deterministically.
- Confirm `PrepareEtaGeneratedReduction(...)` preserves generated-target order, emits eta-shifted family and kinematics files, rejects empty generated target lists, and feeds cleanly into the existing fake-execution boundary.
- Confirm `PrepareInvariantGeneratedReduction(...)` preserves generated-target order, emits original-spec family and kinematics files without eta insertion, rejects empty generated target lists, and feeds cleanly into the existing fake-execution boundary.
- Confirm the invariant-name `PrepareInvariantGeneratedReduction(...)` overload composes `BuildInvariantDerivativeSeed(...)` with the existing seed-based preparation path and preserves both the seed-builder diagnostics and the existing master-basis validation surface.
- Confirm `RunEtaGeneratedReduction(...)` returns populated parsed/assembled results only after reducer execution succeeds and the parsed results assemble successfully.
- Confirm `RunEtaGeneratedReduction(...)` parses reducer outputs from the recorded execution working-directory artifact root instead of assuming `layout.root`.
- Confirm eta-generated wrapper failures preserve execution status/logs on reducer failure and reject identity-fallback parsed reductions for generated eta targets.
- Confirm `BuildEtaGeneratedDESystem(...)` reuses the reviewed `RunEtaGeneratedReduction(...)` wrapper, returns the assembled `DESystem` unchanged on success, and converts unsuccessful reducer runs into deterministic consumer-level failures without altering eta preparation, execution, or assembly behavior.
- Confirm the invariant-name `RunInvariantGeneratedReduction(...)` overload reuses the reviewed automatic preparation seam and then routes through the same post-preparation execution, parsing, and assembly path as the seed-based overload.
- Confirm automatic invariant execution preserves the original family/kinematics YAML without eta insertion, preserves generated-target order, and parses reducer outputs from the recorded execution working-directory artifact root using the original family name.
- Confirm automatic invariant execution preserves the reviewed preparation and assembly diagnostics for empty invariant names, unsupported scalar-rule grammar, master-basis mismatches, empty generated target lists, identity-fallback results, and missing explicit rules for generated targets.
- Confirm `BuildInvariantGeneratedDESystem(...)` reuses the reviewed automatic `RunInvariantGeneratedReduction(...)` wrapper, returns the assembled `DESystem` unchanged on success, and converts unsuccessful reducer runs into deterministic consumer-level failures without altering reducer orchestration behavior.
- Confirm `SolveInvariantGeneratedSeries(...)` reuses `BuildInvariantGeneratedDESystem(...)`, forwards `start_location`, `target_location`, `PrecisionPolicy`, and `requested_digits` unchanged into `SolveRequest`, returns `SolverDiagnostics` unchanged, and never calls the solver when upstream automatic invariant `DESystem` construction fails.
- Confirm `SolveEtaGeneratedSeries(...)` reuses `BuildEtaGeneratedDESystem(...)`, forwards `start_location`, `target_location`, `PrecisionPolicy`, and `requested_digits` unchanged into `SolveRequest`, returns `SolverDiagnostics` unchanged, and never calls the solver when upstream eta `DESystem` construction fails.
- Confirm `SolveEtaModePlannedSeries(...)` reuses `EtaMode::Plan(...)` plus `SolveEtaGeneratedSeries(...)`, preserves planning and downstream eta diagnostics unchanged, forwards solver request fields unchanged, and never calls the solver when planning or eta `DESystem` construction fails.
- Confirm `SolveBuiltinEtaModeSeries(...)` reuses `MakeBuiltinEtaMode(...)` plus `SolveEtaModePlannedSeries(...)`, preserves builtin-name resolution, planning, and downstream eta diagnostics unchanged, forwards solver request fields unchanged, and never calls the solver when builtin resolution, planning, or eta `DESystem` construction fails.
- Confirm `SolveBuiltinEtaModeListSeries(...)` uses the caller-supplied builtin-name order for planning selection, preserves empty-list and unknown-name validation at the wrapper boundary, delegates exactly once through `SolveBuiltinEtaModeSeries(...)` after the first planning-successful builtin is found, and does not fall through to later builtin names after downstream eta `DESystem` construction has started.
- Confirm the builtin overload of `SolveAmfOptionsEtaModeSeries(...)` still uses only
  `amf_options.amf_modes` for ordered builtin selection, preserves the reviewed ordered
  builtin-list diagnostics unchanged, keeps the narrow `UseCache` / `SkipReduction` wrapper
  semantics, and after eta-mode selection rebuilds the live wrapper-owned solve policy from
  `WorkingPre`, `ChopPre`, `XOrder`, `ExtraXOrder`, `LearnXOrder`, `TestXOrder`,
  `RationalizePre`, and `RunLength`, while also threading `amf_options.d0` into
  `SolveRequest.amf_requested_d0` plus the derived
  `amf_requested_dimension_expression`.
- Confirm `ResolveEtaMode(...)` preserves builtin resolution when no user-defined mode claims the queried name, returns the exact registered user-defined mode instance for a unique non-builtin match, rejects null/duplicate/colliding user-defined registrations deterministically, and does not widen current solver wrappers or `AmfOptions` behavior.
- Confirm `SolveResolvedEtaModeSeries(...)` reuses `ResolveEtaMode(...)` plus `SolveEtaModePlannedSeries(...)`, preserves resolution, planning, and downstream eta diagnostics unchanged, forwards solver request fields unchanged, and never calls the solver when resolution, planning, or eta `DESystem` construction fails.
- Confirm `SolveResolvedEtaModeListSeries(...)` uses the caller-supplied mixed name order for planning selection, preserves empty-list and resolver-validation diagnostics at the wrapper boundary, treats standard `EtaMode::Plan(...)` failures as ordered fallback misses, carries the winning planned decision forward without re-planning the selected mode, and does not fall through to later names after downstream eta `DESystem` construction has started.
- Confirm the mixed overload of `SolveAmfOptionsEtaModeSeries(...)` still uses only
  `amf_options.amf_modes` for ordered mixed builtin/user-defined selection, preserves the
  reviewed mixed-list diagnostics unchanged, keeps the narrow `UseCache` / `SkipReduction`
  wrapper semantics, and after eta-mode selection rebuilds the same live wrapper-owned solve
  policy from `WorkingPre`, `ChopPre`, `XOrder`, `ExtraXOrder`, `LearnXOrder`, `TestXOrder`,
  `RationalizePre`, and `RunLength`, while also threading `amf_options.d0` into
  `SolveRequest.amf_requested_d0` plus the derived
  `amf_requested_dimension_expression`.
- Confirm the newly live wrapper-owned runtime-policy fields and narrow current wrapper-owned
  `D0` metadata participate in the same deterministic runtime surfaces as other live wrapper
  inputs: the solver-owned `SolveRequest` policy/metadata surface, solved-path cache slotting
  plus request fingerprinting, solved-path request-summary truthfulness, and `skip_reduction`
  replay validation when request fingerprints are compared.
- Confirm `ResolveEndingScheme(...)` validates the full supplied user-defined registry for null entries, duplicate names, and builtin-name collisions before any lookup proceeds, preserves builtin resolution when no user-defined scheme claims the queried name, and returns the exact registered user-defined scheme instance for a unique non-builtin match.
- Confirm `PlanEndingScheme(...)` reuses `ResolveEndingScheme(...)` plus `EndingScheme::Plan(...)`, preserves resolution and planning diagnostics unchanged, does not mutate the input `ProblemSpec`, and remains uncoupled from boundary providers or solver execution.
- Confirm builtin ending-scheme planning remains the accepted Phase A placeholder surface only: `terminal_strategy` mirrors the selected builtin name, `terminal_nodes` always includes `<family>::eta->infinity`, only builtin `Trivial` adds `<family>::trivial-region`, and no row claims fuller upstream ending semantics yet.
- Confirm `PlanEndingSchemeList(...)` uses the caller-supplied mixed name order for planning selection, preserves empty-list and resolver-validation diagnostics at the wrapper boundary, treats standard `EndingScheme::Plan(...)` failures as ordered fallback misses, carries the winning `EndingDecision` forward without re-planning the selected scheme, and preserves the final planning diagnostic unchanged when the list exhausts.
- Confirm `PlanAmfOptionsEndingScheme(...)` reads only `amf_options.ending_schemes`, forwards that vector unchanged into `PlanEndingSchemeList(...)`, preserves all reviewed ending-selection diagnostics unchanged, and does not let any non-`ending_schemes` `AmfOptions` field affect selection or result shape.
- Confirm `Batch 32` removes `DESystem`-owned boundary storage from the public solver surface and introduces a typed `BoundaryRequest` validation boundary instead of relying on `DESystem.boundaries`.
- Confirm `Batch 33` keeps manual boundary attachment explicit, surfaces missing or incompatible explicit boundary data as typed `boundary_unsolved` before solver execution, and does not widen into automatic boundary providers, ending-coupled generation, or later solver semantics.
- Confirm `Batch 44` adds only a caller-supplied provider seam over the existing boundary surface: it validates `boundary_requests` before provider use, enforces provider/request strategy agreement, calls `Provide(...)` once per request in request order, routes provider output back through `AttachManualBoundaryConditions(...)`, and does not change `BootstrapSeriesSolver`, `SolveDifferentialEquation(...)`, ending coupling, builtin `eta -> infinity` behavior, registries, or CLI work.
- Confirm `Batch 45` keeps builtin `eta -> infinity` generation pure: it validates `ProblemSpec` before `eta_symbol`, returns exactly one request on the `Standard` plus mass-exact-`"0"` subset, reports unsupported well-formed specs as typed `boundary_unsolved`, and does not couple to `EndingDecision`, provider execution, boundary values, solver calls, or CLI work.
- Confirm `Batch 46` keeps ending-planned eta->infinity generation narrow: it calls `PlanEndingScheme(...)` exactly once, succeeds only for the exact singleton supported terminal node `<family>::eta->infinity`, preserves ordinary ending-resolution/planning diagnostics unchanged, returns the exact Batch 45 request shape with strategy `builtin::eta->infinity`, and still does not widen into ordered ending-list / `AmfOptions` wrappers, provider execution, boundary-value generation, `SolveRequest` construction, solver execution, or CLI work.
- Confirm `Batch 34` evaluates the current coefficient-string grammar exactly at one explicit substitution point, returns canonical exact rationals without mutating stored `DESystem` strings, rejects unresolved symbols / malformed expressions / unknown variables deterministically, and treats division by zero as plain evaluation failure without singular-point classification.
- Confirm `GenerateUpperTriangularRegularPointSeriesPatch(...)` reuses the Batch 36 exact center resolution, basis construction, and regular-center fallback on a full-matrix constant probe, requires a square selected matrix dimension-matched to `masters.size()`, rejects any surviving strictly lower-triangular local support through the requested order, returns identity-normalized exact `C_k` matrices via `(n+1) C_{n+1} = sum_{m=0}^n A_m C_{n-m}`, and keeps dense-matrix support, overlap matching, continuation, and `BootstrapSeriesSolver` replacement deferred.
- Confirm `BootstrapSeriesSolver::Solve(...)` now requires exactly one declared system variable plus explicit manual start-boundary attachment, parses start/target and boundary values exactly, uses fixed order `4` with deterministic `match = (start + target) / 2` and `check = (3*start + target) / 4`, preserves the reviewed Batch 39 regular-only path unchanged, admits only the implemented Batch 43 regular-start -> regular-singular-target mixed path on the upper-triangular integer-exponent Frobenius subset, keeps Frobenius residual and handoff checks internal, returns `boundary_unsolved` for missing/incompatible explicit start boundaries, returns `unsupported_solver_path` for unsupported or inexact one-hop paths, and leaves `PrecisionPolicy` / `requested_digits` unused on the reviewed/implemented exact subset.
- Confirm `SolveDifferentialEquation(const SolveRequest&)` constructs the default solver via `MakeBootstrapSeriesSolver()`, returns `Solve(request)` unchanged, preserves malformed-input exceptions plus reviewed Batch 39 well-formed diagnostics unchanged, does not mutate the caller request, and does not widen injected wrappers or solver semantics.
- Confirm verification commands and results are recorded before the batch is advanced.
